F I B O Q J M Z ^ioeIo1XV

Symmetric Cipher ^6yFevDop

Plaintext ^4CETWLqp

Key ^Cjmt3O57

Any encryption algorithm
where the same key is used
to encrypt and decrypt ^nCcZTYl7

and ^FaHoihdR

A special substitution cipher where each byte is replaced with
another byte. ^HXyUZcUq

They use the S-Box to determine what to replace with ^rSdnIore

4. Mix Columns ^GFaEFDrF

Goal is to diffuse information.

For each column, there is an expression for how to
combine its 4bytes to get a new value for each byte ^ONf6nyOR

A is evaluated first, then B, then C, then D.
subsequent bytes are dependent on the previous byte's value ^FHwhtqxI
